// =============================================================================
// Function Class: Show/Hide product promotions & special offers link
// =============================================================================

function showElement(id) {
  var elm = document.getElementById(id);
  if (elm) {
    elm.style.visibility = 'visible';
    if (elm.getAttribute('name') == 'heroQuickPromoDiv') {
      elm.style.display = 'block';
    }
  }
}
function hideElement(id) {
  var elm = document.getElementById(id);
  if (elm) {
    elm.style.visibility = 'hidden';
    if (elm.getAttribute('name') == 'heroQuickPromoDiv') {
      elm.style.display = 'none';
    }
  }
}
function showHideElement(h_id, div_id) {
  var hiddenTag = document.getElementById(h_id);
  if (hiddenTag) {
    showElement(div_id);
  } else {
    hideElement(div_id);
  }
}

  function tryInitClientTriggeredWeblabs(issInitObj) {
    
    if (opts.isDoCtw) {
      $SearchJS.importEvent('search-csl');
      $SearchJS.when('search-csl').run('autocomplete-csl-init', function delegateToInitSearchCsl(searchCSL) { initSearchCsl( searchCSL, issInitObj ); } );
    } else {
      $SearchJS.declare('canCreateAutocomplete', issInitObj);
    }
  }

  
  
  function initSearchCsl(searchCSL, issInitObject) {
    searchCSL.init(opts.pageType, (window.ue && window.ue.rid) || opts.requestId);

    
    var keydownCtw = opts.keydownTriggeredWeblabs;
    var displayCtw = opts.displayTriggeredWeblabs;

    
    issInitObject.doCTWKeydown = function(e) {
        for (var i = 0; i < keydownCtw.length; i++) {
          searchCSL.addWlt(keydownCtw[i].call ? keydownCtw[i](e) : keydownCtw[i]);
        }
      };

    issInitObject.doCTWDisplay = function(data) {
        for (var i = 0; i < displayCtw.length; i++) {
          searchCSL.addWlt(displayCtw[i].call ? displayCtw[i](data) : displayCtw[i]);
        }
      };

    $SearchJS.declare('canCreateAutocomplete', issInitObject);
  } // END initSearchCsl

  
  
  function createAutocomplete(issObject) {
    iss = new AutoComplete(issObject);

    $SearchJS.publish('search-js-autocomplete', iss);

    logMetrics();
  } // END createAutocomplete

  
  
  function buildIssInitObject(opts, issOpts, isNewIss) {
    var issInitObj = {
        src: opts.host
      , mkt: opts.marketId
      , obfMkt: opts.obfuscatedMarketId
      , aliases: opts.searchAliases
      , fb: issOpts.fallbackFlag
      , isDigitalFeaturesEnabled: issOpts.isDigitalFeaturesEnabled
      , isWayfindingEnabled: issOpts.isWayfindingEnabled
      , issPrimeEligible: issOpts.issPrimeEligible
      , deptText: issOpts.departmentText
      , sugText: issOpts.suggestionText
      , filterAliases: opts.filterAliases
      , cf: issOpts.cf
      , ime: opts.isJpOrCn
      , mktid: opts.marketId
      , qs: opts.isJpOrCn
      , issCorpus: issOpts.issCorpus
      , deepNodeISS: {
          searchAliasAccessor: function($) {
            return (window.SearchPageAccess && window.SearchPageAccess.searchAlias()) ||
                   $('select.searchSelect').children().attr('data-root-alias');
          },
          searchAliasDisplayNameAccessor: function() {
            return (window.SearchPageAccess && window.SearchPageAccess.searchAliasDisplayName());
          }
        }
    };

    // If we aren't using the new ISS then we need to add these properties
    if (!isNewIss) {
      issInitObj.dd = issOpts.dropdown; // The element with id searchDropdownBox doesn't exist in C.
      issInitObj.imeSpacing = issOpts.imeSpacing;
      issInitObj.isNavInline = 1;
      issInitObj.triggerISSOnClick = 0;
      issInitObj.sc = 1;
      issInitObj.np = issOpts.np;
    }

    return issInitObj;
  } // END buildIssInitObject

    }
  } // END logMetrics

<div id="bbop-sbbop-container" class="a-section">
    
        
        <div id="sbbop-popover-header" class="a-section a-hidden">
            <div class="a-box a-alert-inline a-alert-inline-success">
                <div class="a-box-inner a-alert-container">
                    <i class="a-icon a-icon-alert"></i>

<script type="text/javascript">


if( window.P ){
    P.when("A").execute(function(A) {

        
        if (window.sbbopLoaded === undefined) {
            window.sbbopLoaded = false;
        }
        

        function getQueryParameterByName(name) {
            name = name.replace(/[\[]/, "\\[").replace(/[\]]/, "\\]");

            var regex = new RegExp("[\\?&]" + name + "=([^&#]*)"),
                results = regex.exec(location.search);

            return results == null ? "" : decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, " "));
        }

        
        var hidden, visibilityChange;
        if (typeof document.hidden !== "undefined") { 
            hidden = "hidden";
            visibilityChange = "visibilitychange";
        } else if (typeof document.mozHidden !== "undefined") {
            hidden = "mozHidden";
            visibilityChange = "mozvisibilitychange";
        } else if (typeof document.msHidden !== "undefined") {
            hidden = "msHidden";
            visibilityChange = "msvisibilitychange";
        } else if (typeof document.webkitHidden !== "undefined") {
            hidden = "webkitHidden";
            visibilityChange = "webkitvisibilitychange";
        }

        
        var loadFeatures = function() {
            

            
            var $ = A.$,
                $container = $("#bbop-sbbop-container");

            var data = {
                "ASIN" : "B00000B5LO",
                "merchantID" : "A3JWKAKR8XB7XF",
                "bbopruleID" : "Acquisition_AddToCart_PrimeBasicFreeTrialUpsellEligible",
                "sbbopruleID" : "Acquisition_AddToCart_PrimeBasicFreeTrialUpsellEligible",
                "deliveryOptions" : "[pri-intl-eu-us-ag,expd-intl-eu-na-ag,std-de-us]",
                "preorder" : "false",
                "releaseDateDeliveryEligible" : "false"
            };

            
            $.get("/gp/product/du/bbop-ms3-ajax-endpoint.html", data, function(result) {
                
                    
                    
                        $container.append(result);
                    
                

                
                
                

                if (getQueryParameterByName("checkBBOP") === "true") {
                    P.when("a-modal", "ready").execute(function(modal) {
                      $('#bbop-check-box').click();
                    });
                }

                
                loadSBBOP();
                
            });

            
            var loadSBBOP = function(){
                P.when("a-modal", "ready").execute(function(modal) {
                    if(!window.sbbopLoaded){
                        var sbbop_modal = createModal(modal);

                        if (sbbop_modal !== undefined) {
                            $(document.body).delegate('#add-to-cart-button','click.sbbop', function(event){
                                $(document.body).undelegate('#add-to-cart-button','click.sbbop');

                                var $sbbop = $("#sbbop-container"),
                                    $sbbopContent = $sbbop.find("#sbbop-popover-content"),
                                    $sbbopHeader = $container.find("#sbbop-popover-header"),
                                    $sbbopFooter = $sbbop.find("#sbbop-popover-footer"),
                                    isAsinizationCase = $sbbop.find(".is-sbbop-asinization-usecase").length > 0,
                                    $bbopCheckbox = $('#bbop-check-box'),
                                    $atcButton = $('#add-to-cart-button'),
                                    atcName = $atcButton.attr("name"),
                                    hasSingleYesButton = ($('#sbbop-yes-button').length === 1),
                                    hasSingleNoButton  = ($('#sbbop-no-button').length === 1),
                                    validAtcButton = ($atcButton.length === 1 && atcName != "submit.add-to-cart-prime-buy-box.x"),
                                    validSbbopContent = ($sbbopContent.length === 1 && $sbbopHeader.length === 1 && $sbbopFooter.length === 1),
                                    validSbbopButtons = (hasSingleYesButton && hasSingleNoButton),
                                    bbopIsNotChecked = !$bbopCheckbox.is(":checked");

                                if (validAtcButton && validSbbopContent && validSbbopButtons && bbopIsNotChecked) {
                                    $atcButton.bind('click.sbbop', function(){return false;});  
                                    $(document.body).delegate("#sbbop-yes-button", "click", function(event){
                                        if(isAsinizationCase){
                                            $bbopCheckbox.prop("checked",true);
                                            logMetric("CSM_prime_surprise_BBOP_yes_button_HO");
                                        }
                                        else {
                                            $atcButton.attr("name", "submit.add-to-cart-prime-buy-box.x");
                                            logMetric("CSM_prime_surprise_BBOP_yes_button");
                                        }
                                        safeATCClick();
                                    });

                                    $(document.body).delegate("#sbbop-no-button", "click", function(event){
                                        if(isAsinizationCase) {
                                            logMetric("CSM_prime_surprise_BBOP_no_button_HO");
                                        }
                                        else {
                                            logMetric("CSM_prime_surprise_BBOP_no_button");
                                        }
                                        safeATCClick();
                                    });

                                    
                                    $(document.body).delegate(".a-popover", "keydown", function(event){
                                        if(event.keyCode == "27"){
                                            event.preventDefault();
                                        }
                                    });

                                    A.on("a:popover:ajaxFail:sbbop_modal", safeATCClick);
                                    A.on("a:popover:hide:sbbop_modal", function(){
                                        if(isAsinizationCase) {
                                            logMetric("CSM_prime_surprise_BBOP_close_button_HO");
                                        }
                                        else {
                                            logMetric("CSM_prime_surprise_BBOP_close_button");
                                        }
                                        safeATCClick();
                                    });
                                    A.on("a:popover:beforeShow:sbbop_modal", function(){
                                            setEventEmbu();
                                    });

                                    sbbop_modal.show();
                                    if(isAsinizationCase) {
                                        logMetric("CSM_prime_surprise_BBOP_presentation_HO");
                                    }
                                    else {
                                        logMetric("CSM_prime_surprise_BBOP_presentation");
                                    }
                                    return false;
                                } 
                            });
                        }
                        window.sbbopLoaded = true;
                    }
                });
            };

            var createModal = function(modal) {
                var $sbbop = $("#sbbop-container"),
                    $sbbopContent = $sbbop.find("#sbbop-popover-content"),
                    $sbbopHeader = $container.find("#sbbop-popover-header"),
                    $sbbopFooter = $sbbop.find("#sbbop-popover-footer");

                if($sbbopContent.length === 1 && $sbbopHeader.length === 1 && $sbbopFooter.length === 1){ 
                    sbbopWidth = parseInt(($sbbop.find("#sbbop-popover")).attr("popover-width"), 10);

                    return modal.create($sbbop, {
                        "inlineContent": $sbbopContent.html(),
                        "header": $sbbopHeader.html(),
                        "footer": $sbbopFooter.html(),
                        "width": sbbopWidth,
                        "activate": "onclick",
                        "name": "sbbop_modal"
                    });
                }
                return undefined;
            }

            var logMetric = function(customTag){
                if(window.ue && ue.tag) {
                    ue.tag(customTag, "surpriseBBOP")
                }
            };

            var postBackMetrics = function(){
                if (window.ue){
                    uex("ld", "surpriseBBOP");
                }
            };

            var setEventEmbu = function(){
                var eventData = { "eventCode" : "106" };
                $.get("/gp/prime/utility/record-embu-event.html", eventData);
            };

            var safeATCClick = function() {
                postBackMetrics();                                 
                $('#add-to-cart-button').unbind('click.sbbop')     
                    .click()                                       
                    .bind('click.sbbop',function(){return false}); 
            };
            
            
        }

        
        var handleVisibilityChange = function() {
            if (!document[hidden]) {
                
                document.removeEventListener(visibilityChange, handleVisibilityChange);
                loadFeatures();
            }
        }

        if (typeof document.addEventListener === "undefined" ||
            typeof document[hidden] === "undefined" || !document[hidden]) {
            
            loadFeatures();
        } else {
            
            document.addEventListener(visibilityChange, handleVisibilityChange);
        }
    });
}
</script>

		<div class="a-fixed-left-grid"><div class="a-fixed-left-grid-inner" style="padding-left:19px">

				<i class="a-icon autorip_logo_small"></i>
			</div>

				Inklusive kostenloser MP3-Version dieses Albums.
			</div>
		</div></div>

    function toggleExpanderHeaderTextWeight(data) {
       $("[data-a-expander-name="+data.expander.expanderName+"] .a-mbc-expander-heading-text").toggleClass("a-mbc-expander-heading-text-bold");
    }

    var offerCount = 0;
    for(var i=1; i <= offerCount; i++){
        $(".mbcLi"+i).bind("click", function(){
            this.click();
        });
        $(".mbcLi"+i+" .a-button a").bind("click", function(){
            window.open(this.href,"_self");
        });
        A.on('a:expander:mbc_expander_'+i+':toggle:expand', toggleExpanderHeaderTextWeight);
        A.on('a:expander:mbc_expander_'+i+':toggle:collapse', toggleExpanderHeaderTextWeight);
    }

    if ($("#mbc-panel").length == 0) {
        $("#mbc-action-panel-wrapper").show();
    }
});

<script type="text/javascript">
maintainHeight = function(){
    var mainHolder = document.getElementById("main-image-container");
    var imgTagWrapperId = document.getElementById("imgTagWrapperId");
    if(mainHolder && typeof mainHolder != 'undefined'){
        var ratio = 1.0;
        var shouldAutoPlay = false;
        var videoSizes = [[355, 315], [450, 400], [425, 377], [466, 414], [522, 464]];
        
        
        var width = mainHolder.offsetWidth;
        var containerHeight = width/ratio;
        containerHeight = Math.min(containerHeight, 700);

        var landingImage = document.getElementById("landingImage");
        var imageHeight = Math.min(containerHeight, 464);
        var imageWidth = Math.min(width, 522);

        

        mainHolder.style.height = containerHeight + "px";
        if(imgTagWrapperId && typeof imgTagWrapperId !== 'undefined' ){
            imgTagWrapperId.style.height = containerHeight + "px";
        }
        if(landingImage){
            landingImage.style.maxHeight = imageHeight + "px";
            landingImage.style.maxWidth  = imageWidth + "px";
        }

        if(shouldAutoPlay){
            if(landingImage){
                var autoPlayWidth=0, autoPlayHeight=0;
                for(var i=0; i < videoSizes.length; i++){
                    if( autoPlayWidth < videoSizes[i][0] ){
                        autoPlayWidth = videoSizes[i][0];
                        autoPlayHeight = videoSizes[i][1];
                    }
                }
                if( autoPlayWidth > 0 && autoPlayHeight > 0 ){
                    var videoRatio = autoPlayWidth/autoPlayHeight;
                    // increasing height of the slate image by 1px (and width with the ratio) so that black lines doesn't appear on ipad on right side.
                    var isIpad = navigator.userAgent.match(/ipad/i);
                    if( isIpad ){
                        containerHeight = containerHeight + 1;
                    }
                    landingImage.style.width = containerHeight * videoRatio + "px";
                    landingImage.style.height = containerHeight + "px";
                }

            }
        }
    }
};
maintainHeight();

window.onresize = function(){
    maintainHeight();
};

            <script type="text/javascript">
P.when("A","jQuery","cf").execute(function(A,$){
    window.registeredDDMCountdown || P.register("DDMCountdownComponent",function() {
        var countdonwHandler;
        return {
            init: function(ddmContext) {
                countdonwHandler || (countdonwHandler = new CountdownHandler(ddmContext));
            },
            start: function(fastSecondsLeftToOrder,cheapSecondsLeftToOrder) {
                countdonwHandler.start(fastSecondsLeftToOrder,cheapSecondsLeftToOrder);
            },
            stop: function() {
                countdonwHandler.stop();
            }
        };
    });
    window.registeredDDMCountdown = true;
    
    function CountdownHandler(ddmContext) {
        var strings = ddmContext.strings;
        var asin = ddmContext.asin;
        var shippingMessageSectionId = ddmContext.shippingMessageSectionId;
        var fastCountdownElementId = ddmContext.fastCountdownElementId;
        var cheapCountdownElementId = ddmContext.cheapCountdownElementId;
        var showAndInCountDown = ddmContext.showAndInCountDown;

        var fastCountdownTimer = null;
        var cheapCountdownTimer = null;

        this.start = function(fastSecondsLeftToOrder,cheapSecondsLeftToOrder) {
            this.stop();
            if (fastCountdownElementId && fastSecondsLeftToOrder > 0) {
                fastCountdownTimer = new CountdownTimer(strings,asin,shippingMessageSectionId,
                        fastCountdownElementId,fastSecondsLeftToOrder,showAndInCountDown);
                fastCountdownTimer.start();
            }
            if (cheapCountdownElementId && cheapSecondsLeftToOrder > 0) {
                cheapCountdownTimer = new CountdownTimer(strings,asin,shippingMessageSectionId,
                        cheapCountdownElementId,cheapSecondsLeftToOrder,showAndInCountDown);
                cheapCountdownTimer.start();
            }
        };
        this.stop = function() {
            if (fastCountdownTimer) {
                fastCountdownTimer.stop();
                fastCountdownTimer = null;
            }
            if (cheapCountdownTimer) {
                cheapCountdownTimer.stop();
                cheapCountdownTimer = null;
            }
        };
    };

    function CountdownTimer(strings, asin, shippingMessageSectionId, countdownElementId, secondsLeft,showAndInCountDown) {
        this.secondsLeft = secondsLeft;
        this.intervalHandle = null;

        this.start = function() {
            var thisObj = this;
            this.intervalHandle = A.interval(function(){
                if (thisObj) {
                    thisObj.updateCountdownText();
                }
            }, 1000);
        };

        this.stop = function() {
            if (this.intervalHandle) {
                window.clearInterval(this.intervalHandle);
            }
        };

        this.updateCountdownText = function() {
            this.secondsLeft --;
            if (this.secondsLeft > 0) {
                var remainMins = Math.floor(this.secondsLeft / 60);
                var minutes = remainMins % 60;
                var hours = Math.floor(remainMins / 60);
                var seconds = this.secondsLeft % 60;
                var hourString   = (hours > 1) ? strings.hours : strings.hour;
                var minuteString = (minutes > 1) ? strings.minutes : strings.minute;
                var secondString = (seconds > 1) ? strings.seconds : strings.second;
                var seperatorString = strings.timeSeperator;
                var andString = strings.and;

                var countdownText;
                if (hours > 0 && minutes > 0) {
                    if (showAndInCountDown) {
                        countdownText = hours + seperatorString + hourString + seperatorString + andString + seperatorString + minutes + seperatorString + minuteString;
                    } else {
                        countdownText = hours + seperatorString + hourString + seperatorString + minutes + seperatorString + minuteString;
                    }
                } else if ( hours > 0 && minutes == 0 ) {
                    countdownText = hours + seperatorString + hourString;
                } else if ( hours == 0 && minutes > 0 ) {
                    countdownText = minutes + seperatorString + minuteString;
                } else {
                    countdownText = seconds + seperatorString + secondString;
                }
                $(countdownElementId).html(countdownText);
            } else {
                this.stop();
                var refreshText = "<a href='/gp/product/"+asin+"'>"+strings.refreshTimeout+"</a>";
                $(shippingMessageSectionId).html(refreshText);
            }
        };
    };
});
</script>

            <script type="text/javascript">
/**
 * Component: used to control other features(buybox,mbc,miniAtf) for Ship By Region.
 */
P.when("A","jQuery","a-popover","cf").execute(function(A,$,popover) {
    window.registeredDDMSBRComponent || P.register("DDMShipByRegionComponent",function() {
        var mbcDataUrl = "/gp/product/features/dynamic-delivery-message/udp-ajax-handler/get-mbc-location-based-data.html?_encoding=UTF-8";
        var asin;
        var isMfn;
        var gotoTopElementId;
        var bbUndeliverableAlert;
        var undeliverableLabel;
        var mbcMerchantIds;
        var mbcOfferIsAgsFlags;
        var sbrBehavior = {
            onlySupportMfn: false,
            updateBuyBtnInBB: false,
            updateShipChargeForMfnInBB: false,
            updateAvailInBB: false,
            showUndeliverablePopInBB: false,
            updateBuyBtnInMBC: false,
            updateShipChargeForMfnInMBC: false,
            updateAvailInMBC: false,
            showUndeliverablePopInMBC: false,
            updateBuyBtnInMiniATF: false,
            updateAvailInMiniATF: false,
            reloadPageWhenBBWinnerChange: false,
            ignoreAgsOfferInMBC: false
        };
        var defaultMbcShipChargeText;
        
        var updateBuyBox = function(isDeliverable,shipChargeText) {
            if (sbrBehavior.onlySupportMfn && !isMfn) return;
        
            sbrBehavior.updateAvailInBB && updateAvailInBB(isDeliverable);
            sbrBehavior.updateShipChargeForMfnInBB && updateShipChargeForMfnInBB(shipChargeText);
            sbrBehavior.updateBuyBtnInBB && updateBuyBtnInBB(isDeliverable);
            sbrBehavior.showUndeliverablePopInBB && updateUndeliverablePopInBB(isDeliverable);
        };
        var updateAvailInBB = function(isDeliverable) {
            if (isDeliverable) {
                $("#soldByThirdParty").show();
            } else {
                $("#soldByThirdParty").hide();
            }
        };
        var updateShipChargeForMfnInBB = function(shipChargeText) {
            if (isMfn && shipChargeText) {
                $("#soldByThirdParty").find("span.shipping3P").html(shipChargeText);
            }
        };
        var updateBuyBtnInBB = function(isDeliverable) {
            $("#buybox\\.addToCart span.a-button-primary").unbind("click");
            $("#buyNow span.a-button-primary").unbind("click");
            if (isDeliverable) {
                // update UI
                $("#submit\\.add-to-cart").removeClass('a-button-disabled');//pc add to cart
                $("#buybox\\.addToCart span.a-button-primary").removeClass('a-button-disabled');//mobile add to cart
                $("#buyNow span.a-button-primary").removeClass('a-button-disabled'); // mobile buy now
                $("#oneClickAvailable span.a-button-oneclick").removeClass('a-button-disabled'); // all device one-click btn
                // enable input
                $("#add-to-cart-button").attr("disabled", false);
                $("#one-click-button").attr("disabled", false); // pc one-click
                $("#buyNow input.a-button-input").attr("disabled", false); // mobile buy now
                //TODO: add-on button
            } else {
                // update UI
                $("#submit\\.add-to-cart").addClass('a-button-disabled');//pc add to cart
                $("#buybox\\.addToCart span.a-button-primary").addClass('a-button-disabled');//mobile add to cart
                $("#buyNow span.a-button-primary").addClass('a-button-disabled'); // mobile buy now
                $("#oneClickAvailable span.a-button-oneclick").addClass('a-button-disabled');// all device one-click btn
                // disable input
                $("#add-to-cart-button").attr("disabled", true);
                $("#one-click-button").attr("disabled", true);
                $("#buyNow input.a-button-input").attr("disabled", true); // mobile buy now
                // disable click event for mobile
                $("#buybox\\.addToCart span.a-button-primary").bind("click",function(){
                    event.stopImmediatePropagation();
                });
                $("#buyNow span.a-button-primary").bind("click",function(){
                    event.stopImmediatePropagation();
                });
            }
        };
        var updateUndeliverablePopInBB = function(isDeliverable) {
            if (isDeliverable) {
                popover.remove($("#submit\\.add-to-cart"));
                popover.remove($("#oneClickAvailable span.a-button-oneclick"));
            } else {
                var content = "<span class='ddm-sbr-undeliverable-alert'>" + bbUndeliverableAlert + "</span>";
                popover.create($("#submit\\.add-to-cart"), {
                    "content": content,
                    "position": "triggerLeft",
                    "closeButton": false
                });
                popover.create($("#oneClickAvailable span.a-button-oneclick"), {
                    "content": content,
                    "position": "triggerLeft",
                    "closeButton": false
                });
            }
        };
        
        var updateMBC = function(address) {
            if (!mbcMerchantIds) return;
            initDefaultMbcShipChargeText();
            
            var mParas = [];
            mParas.push("asin=" + asin);
            address.zipCode && mParas.push("zipCode=" + address.zipCode);
            address.state && mParas.push("state=" + address.state);
            address.city && mParas.push("city=" + address.city);
            address.district && mParas.push("district=" + address.district);
            address.countryCode && mParas.push("countryCode=" + address.countryCode);
            address.useDefaultShippingAddress && mParas.push("useDefaultShippingAddress=" + address.useDefaultShippingAddress);
            
            var mbcElementCount = mbcMerchantIds.length;
            for (var i=1; i<= mbcElementCount; i++) {
                mParas.push("m" + i + "=" + mbcMerchantIds[i-1]);
            }

            if (mbcElementCount > 0) {
                $.ajax({
                    type: "POST",
                    url: mbcDataUrl,
                    contentType: 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded;charset=utf-8',
                    data: mParas.join('&'),
                    dataType: "json",
                    success: function(data){
                        var shipChargeElements = $("#mbc div.mbc-offer-row span.a-color-price ~ span");
                        var addToCartElements = $("#mbc div.mbc-offer-row span.a-button.a-button-primary");
                        var popoverElements = $("#mbc div.mbc-offer-row span.a-declarative");
                
                        if (data && data.infoList 
                                && data.infoList.length == mbcElementCount
                                && shipChargeElements && addToCartElements && popoverElements
                                && mbcElementCount == shipChargeElements.length
                                && mbcElementCount == addToCartElements.length
                                && mbcElementCount == popoverElements.length) {
                            for(var i = 0; i < mbcElementCount; i ++) {
                                var mbcItem = data.infoList[i];
                                var mid = mbcItem.merchantID;
                                if (mid && mid === mbcMerchantIds[i]
                                        && mbcItem.enableSBR
                                        && (!sbrBehavior.onlySupportMfn || mbcItem.isMfn)
                                        && !(sbrBehavior.ignoreAgsOfferInMBC
                                                && mbcOfferIsAgsFlags != null
                                                && mbcElementCount == mbcOfferIsAgsFlags.length
                                                && mbcOfferIsAgsFlags[i] === "1")) {

                                    // update ship charge
                                    if (sbrBehavior.updateShipChargeForMfnInMBC) {
                                        var shipChargeText = mbcItem.shipChargeText;
                                        if (mbcItem.isDeliverable) {
                                            shipChargeText = mbcItem.isMfn && shipChargeText ? shipChargeText : defaultMbcShipChargeText[mid];
                                        } else {
                                            shipChargeText = undeliverableLabel;
                                        }
                                        
                                        $(shipChargeElements[i]).html(shipChargeText);
                                    }
                                    
                                    // update buy button
                                    if (sbrBehavior.updateBuyBtnInMBC) {
                                        var $addToCartBtn = $(addToCartElements[i]);
                                        $addToCartBtn.find("a").unbind("click");
                                        if (mbcItem.isDeliverable) {
                                            $addToCartBtn.removeClass("a-button-disabled");
                                        } else {
                                            $addToCartBtn.addClass("a-button-disabled");
                                            $addToCartBtn.find("a").bind("click", function(event) {
                                                event.preventDefault();
                                            });
                                        }
                                    }
                                    
                                    // update popover
                                    if (sbrBehavior.showUndeliverablePopInMBC) {
                                        var $popoverTrigger = $(popoverElements[i]);
                                        var popoverParam = $popoverTrigger.attr("data-a-popover");
                                        if(popoverParam) {
                                            popover.remove($popoverTrigger);
                                            if (mbcItem.isDeliverable) {
                                               popoverParam = eval("[" + popoverParam + "]");
                                                popover.create($popoverTrigger, popoverParam[0]);
                                            } else {
                                               popover.create($popoverTrigger, {
                                                    "content" : "<span class='ddm-sbr-undeliverable-alert'>" + bbUndeliverableAlert + "</span>",
                                                    "position" : "triggerLeft",
                                                    "closeButton" : false
                                                });
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        };
        var initDefaultMbcShipChargeText = function() {
            if (!defaultMbcShipChargeText) {
                defaultMbcShipChargeText = {};
                var currentShipChargeText = $("#mbc div.mbc-offer-row span.a-color-price ~ span.a-color-secondary");
                
                if(currentShipChargeText && mbcMerchantIds && currentShipChargeText.length == mbcMerchantIds.length) {
                    for(var i=0; i < mbcMerchantIds.length; i++) {
                        defaultMbcShipChargeText[mbcMerchantIds[i]] = $(currentShipChargeText[i]).html();
                    }
                }
            }
        };
        
        var updateMiniAtf = function(isDeliverable,miniAvailText) {
            if (sbrBehavior.onlySupportMfn && !isMfn) return;

            if (miniAvailText) {
                A.delay(function(){
                    // update avail msg
                    if (sbrBehavior.updateAvailInMiniATF) {
                        $("#gTTLink div.availability-shipping span.scarcity").html(miniAvailText);
                        gotoTopElementId && $(gotoTopElementId).click(function(event){
                            jQuery("#gTTLink").slideUp();
                            jQuery("body,html").animate({scrollTop: 0}, 300);
                            event.stopImmediatePropagation();
                        });
                    }
                    // update buy button
                    if (sbrBehavior.updateBuyBtnInMiniATF) {
                        var $miniAtfBuyBtn = $("#gTTLink div.add-to-cart");
                        $miniAtfBuyBtn.find("span.a-button-primary a").unbind("click");
                        if (isDeliverable) {
                            $miniAtfBuyBtn.find("button.a-button-text").attr("disabled", false);
                            $miniAtfBuyBtn.find("span.a-button-primary").removeClass('a-button-disabled');
                        } else {
                            $miniAtfBuyBtn.find("button.a-button-text").attr("disabled", true);
                            $miniAtfBuyBtn.find("span.a-button-primary").addClass('a-button-disabled');
                            $miniAtfBuyBtn.find("span.a-button-primary a").bind("click",function(event){
                                event.preventDefault();
                            });
                        }
                    }
                },1500);
            }
        };
        
        return {
            init: function(ddmContext) {
                asin = ddmContext.asin;
                isMfn = ddmContext.isMfn;
                bbUndeliverableAlert = ddmContext.strings.bbUndeliverableAlert;
                undeliverableLabel = ddmContext.strings.undeliverableLabel;
                gotoTopElementId = ddmContext.sbrContext.gotoTopElementId;
                mbcMerchantIds = ddmContext.sbrContext.mbcMerchantIds;
                mbcOfferIsAgsFlags = ddmContext.sbrContext.mbcOfferIsAgsFlags;
                sbrBehavior = ddmContext.sbrContext.sbrBehavior ? ddmContext.sbrContext.sbrBehavior : sbrBehavior;
                defaultMbcShipChargeText = null;
            },
            updateSBRRelevant: function(selectedAddress,isDeliverable,enableSBR,shipChargeText,miniAvailText,isbbWinnerChanged) {
                if (!enableSBR) return;
                if (sbrBehavior.reloadPageWhenBBWinnerChange && isbbWinnerChanged) {
                    var url = window.location.toString();
                    url = url.split('#')[0];
                    window.location.href = url;
                } else {
                    updateBuyBox(isDeliverable, shipChargeText);
                    updateMBC(selectedAddress);
                    updateMiniAtf(isDeliverable,miniAvailText);
                }
            }
        };
    });
    window.registeredDDMSBRComponent = true;
});
</script>

            <script type="text/javascript">
P.when("A","jQuery","a-popover","DDMShipByRegionComponent","cf").execute(function(A,$,popover,sbrComp){
    window.registeredDDMAddressSelect || P.register("DDMAddressSelectComponent",function() {
        var addressSelectHandler;
        return {
            init: function(ddmContext,countdownComp) {
                addressSelectHandler && addressSelectHandler.destroy();
                (addressSelectHandler = new EUAddressSelectHandler(ddmContext,countdownComp)).init();
            },
            reload: function() {
                addressSelectHandler.reloadDeliveryMessage();
            }
        };
    });
    window.registeredDDMAddressSelect = true;
    /**
    * Function: used to control the address select work flow
    */
    function EUAddressSelectHandler(ddmContext,countdownComp) {
        var isInit = false;
        var isUnifiedLocation = ddmContext.isUnifiedLocation;
        var deviceType = ddmContext.deviceType;
        var selectedCountryCode = ddmContext.selectedCountryCode;
        var strings = ddmContext.strings;
        var asin = ddmContext.asin;
        var preselectedMerchantId = ddmContext.preselectedMerchantId;
        var merchantId = ddmContext.merchantId;
        var shippingMessageSectionId = ddmContext.shippingMessageSectionId;
        var popupName = ddmContext.addressPopover.name;
        var popupType = ddmContext.addressPopover.type;
        var popupTriggerId = ddmContext.popupTriggerId;
        var defaultShippingCountryCode = ddmContext.defaultShippingCountryCode;
        var sbrContext = ddmContext.sbrContext;
        var popupInstance = null;
        var countryOptionHtml = null;
        var countryDataUrl = "/gp/product/features/dynamic-delivery-message/udp-ajax-handler/get-eu-country-data.html?_encoding=UTF-8";
        var updateDeliveryMessageUrl = "/gp/product/features/dynamic-delivery-message/udp-ajax-handler/get-delivery-message.html?_encoding=UTF-8";
        var LOC_UX_ADDRESS_CHANGE_EVENT = "DeliveryAddressDropdown_OnAddressChange";

        this.init = function () {
            if (isInit) return;
            
            if(isUnifiedLocation) {
                A.on(LOC_UX_ADDRESS_CHANGE_EVENT, function(data) {
                    updateDeliveryMessage(0,"",0);
                });
            } else {
                A.on("a:popover:beforeShow:" + popupName, function(data) {
                    loadCountryOptions();
                });
                $(document).delegate(popupTriggerId, "click", function(event){
                    var popupParams = {
                        "name": popupName,
                        "position": "triggerBottom",
                        "closeButton": false,
                        "activate": "onclick"
                    };
                    if(popupInstance) {
                        popupParams.content = popupInstance.getContent();
                        popover.remove(popupInstance);
                    }
                    popupInstance = popover.create($(popupTriggerId), popupParams);
                    popupInstance && popupInstance.show();
                });
                $(document).delegate("#ddmCountryUpdateBtn", "click", function(event){
                    var countryCode = $("#ddmCountrySelect").val();
                    countryCode && updateDeliveryMessage(1,countryCode,0);
                });
                $(document).delegate("#ddmCustomerAddress", "click", function(event){
                    if(defaultShippingCountryCode) {
                        // for Mobile and Tablet
                        $("#ddmCountrySelect li.a-active").removeClass("a-active");
                        $("li#ddmCustomerAddress").addClass("a-active");
                        
                        updateDeliveryMessage(1,defaultShippingCountryCode,1);
                    }
                });
                $(document).delegate("#ddmCountrySelect li", "click", function(event){
                    var countryCode = $(this).attr("countryCode");
                    if (countryCode) {
                        $("#ddmCustomerAddress").removeClass("a-active");
                        $("#ddmCountrySelect li.a-active").removeClass("a-active");
                        $(this).addClass("a-active");
                        updateDeliveryMessage(1,countryCode,0);
                    }
                });
            }
            
            // init sbr component
            initShipByRegionComponent();
            
            isInit = true;
        };
        this.reloadDeliveryMessage = function() {
            $(shippingMessageSectionId).hide();
            updateDeliveryMessage(0,"",0);
        };
        this.destroy = function() {
            if (!isUnifiedLocation) {
                popupInstance && popover.remove(popupInstance);
                $(document).undelegate(popupTriggerId);
                $(document).undelegate("#ddmCountryUpdateBtn");
                $(document).undelegate("#ddmCustomerAddress");
                $(document).undelegate("#ddmCountrySelect li");                
            }
        };
        var loadCountryOptions = function() {
            if (!countryOptionHtml) {
                $.ajax({
                    url: countryDataUrl,
                    data: {"deviceType": deviceType,
                           "selectedCountryCode": selectedCountryCode,
                           "defaultShippingCountryCode": defaultShippingCountryCode ? defaultShippingCountryCode : "",
                           "asin":asin, 
                           "preselectedMerchantId":preselectedMerchantId,
                           "merchantId":(!preselectedMerchantId && !(sbrContext.sbrBehavior && sbrContext.sbrBehavior.reloadPageWhenBBWinnerChange) ? merchantId : "")},
                    dataType: "html",
                    success: function(data){
                        if (data) {
                            countryOptionHtml = data;
                            $("#ddmCountrySelect").html(countryOptionHtml);
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        };
        var showVhvFeature = function() {
            $("#veryHighValueMessage").removeClass("a-hidden");
        };
        var hideVhvFeature = function() {
            $("#veryHighValueMessage").addClass("a-hidden");
        };
        var initShipByRegionComponent = function() {
            sbrComp.init(ddmContext);
            sbrComp.updateSBRRelevant({countryCode: selectedCountryCode}, 
                    ddmContext.isDeliverable, sbrContext.enableSBR, sbrContext.shipChargeText,
                    sbrContext.miniAvailText,false);
        };
        var updateDeliveryMessage = function(updateSembu,countryCode,useDefaultShippingAddress) {
            countdownComp.stop();
            
            if (!isUnifiedLocation) {
                P.when(popupType).execute(function(popup) {
                    popup.get(popupName) && popup.get(popupName).hide();
                });
            }
            
            var canReload = sbrContext.sbrBehavior && sbrContext.sbrBehavior.reloadPageWhenBBWinnerChange;
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: updateDeliveryMessageUrl,
                data: {"asin": asin, 
                       "deviceType": deviceType,
                       "preselectedMerchantId":(canReload ? ddmContext.preselectedMerchantId : ""),
                       "merchantId":(canReload ? "" : ddmContext.merchantId),
                       "updateSembu": updateSembu,
                       "countryCode": countryCode,
                       "useDefaultShippingAddress": useDefaultShippingAddress
                },
                dataType: "json",
                success: function(data){
                    // for Mobile and Tablet
                    $("#ddmSelectedAddressText").html(data.selectedCountryName);
                    selectedCountryCode = data.selectedCountryCode;
                    if (data.template == "deliverable_message") {
                        $("#ddmShippingMessage").html(data.fastShippingMessage);
                        // only display shipping message when fast-trackable on mobile
                        $("#ddmDetailMessage").html(
                                (data.isRdd || data.fastTrackable && data.fastSecondsLeftToOrder > 0) ? 
                                        data.fastShippingMessage : data.helpLink);
                        $("#ddmEligibilityMessage").html(strings.deliverableTo);
                        countdownComp.start(data.fastSecondsLeftToOrder,0);
                        $("#holidayAvailabilityMessage_feature_div").html(data.hamString);
                        $("#holidayDeliveryMessage_feature_div").html(data.hdmString);
                        showVhvFeature();
                    } else {
                        $("#ddmShippingMessage").html(data.undeliverableMessage);
                        $("#ddmEligibilityMessage").html(strings.undeliverableTo);
                        $("#ddmDetailMessage").html(data.helpLink);
                        $("#holidayAvailabilityMessage_feature_div").html("");
                        $("#holidayDeliveryMessage_feature_div").html("");
                        hideVhvFeature();
                    }
                    $(shippingMessageSectionId).show();
                    sbrComp.updateSBRRelevant({countryCode:countryCode},
                            data.isDeliverable,data.enableSBR,data.shipChargeText,
                            data.miniAvailText,false);
                },
                error: function(){
                    $("#dynamicDeliveryMessage").replaceWith(strings.serverBusy);
                    $("#holidayAvailabilityMessage_feature_div").html("");
                    $("#holidayDeliveryMessage_feature_div").html("");
                }
            });
        };
    };
});
</script>

            <script type="text/javascript">
/**
 * Component: used to create fba popover
 */
P.when("A","jQuery","a-popover","cf").execute(function(A,$,popover) {

            <script type="text/javascript">
P.when("A","jQuery","cf").execute(function(A,$){
    window.registeredDDMTwisterHandler || P.register("DDMTwisterHandlerComponent",function() {
        return {
            init: function(ddmContext,addressSelectComp){
                var asin = ddmContext.asin;
                var ddmPageStateData = A.state("ddmPageStateData");
                var visitedAsins = ddmPageStateData ? ddmPageStateData.visitedAsins : null;
                if (visitedAsins) {
                    var isVisited = false;
                    var i = visitedAsins.length;
                    while (i--) {
                        if (visitedAsins[i] == asin) {
                            isVisited = true;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                    if (isVisited) {
                        addressSelectComp.reload();
                    } else {
                        visitedAsins.push(asin);
                        ddmPageStateData.visitedAsins = visitedAsins;
                        A.state("ddmPageStateData",ddmPageStateData);
                    }
                }
            }
        };
    });
    window.registeredDDMTwisterHandler = true;
});
</script>

            <script type="text/javascript">
P.when("A","DDMCountdownComponent","DDMAddressSelectComponent","DDMFbaPopupComponent","DDMTwisterHandlerComponent").execute(
    function(A,countdownComp,addrSelectComp,fbaPopupComp,twisterHandlerComp) {
        window.registeredDDMController || P.register("DDMControllerComponent",function() {
            return {
                run: function(ddmContext) {
                    A.state("ddmPageStateData") || A.state("ddmPageStateData",{
                        visitedAsins: [],
                        selectedAddressText: ddmContext.selectedAddressText
                    });

                    countdownComp.init(ddmContext);
                    countdownComp.start(ddmContext.fastSecondsLeftToOrder,ddmContext.cheapSecondsLeftToOrder);

                    ddmContext.canSelectAddress && addrSelectComp.init(ddmContext,countdownComp);
                    
                    ddmContext.ssofPopover && ddmContext.ssofPopover.show && fbaPopupComp.init(ddmContext);
                    
                    ddmContext.canSelectAddress && twisterHandlerComp.init(ddmContext,addrSelectComp);
                }
            };
        });
        window.registeredDDMController = true;
    }
);
</script>

                 <h2 class="default">Produktbeschreibungen</h2>
                
                
                

            
            
                
                
                  





    <div id="productDescription" class="a-section a-spacing-small prodDescWidth">
        





  
    
  


        
        
     
	       
     
                              
     
       	       
        
        <!-- show up to 2 reviews by default --> 
        
        	
        		<h3>Produktbeschreibungen</h3>
        	
        	
        		
        			<p>BUENA VISTA SOCIAL CLUB
				    	
					</p>
        		
        		
        	
        
        	
        		<h3>Amazon.de</h3>
        	
        	
        		
        			<p>Ry Cooders Name hat nat&#xFC;rlich geholfen, die Aufmerksamkeit auf diese Platte zu lenken, doch es sind die erfahrenen kubanischen Son-Musiker, die dieses Album zu etwas Besonderem machen. In der Themenwahl und dem Gef&#xFC;hl f&#xFC;r ged&#xE4;mpfte Romantik erinnert das Album an Ellington. <P> Wir finden auf <I>Buena Vista Social Club</I> die seltene Verschmelzung von Ruhe und Intensit&#xE4;t. Die Kl&#xE4;nge sind ganz gelassen, und die Spieler stellen eine lebendige Musik in den Vordergrund, die uns daran erinnert, da&#xDF; man auch im Alter nicht auf Lebendigkeit verzichten mu&#xDF;. Barbarito Torres' lautes Solo in "El Cuarto de Tula" ist sowohl bewundernswerter als auch geschmackvoller als jedes Gitarrenst&#xFC;ck auf jedem beliebigen neueren Rock-Album. Eine Version von "Stormy Weather" und einige sehr deutliche Parallelen zu hawaiianischen Stilen erinnern den H&#xF6;rer daran, da&#xDF; dies "World Music" ist. <I>--Rickey Wright</I>
				    	
					</p>
        		
        		
        	
        
                
        
        
            
            <a class="a-link-normal" href="/dp/product-description/B00000B5LO/ref=dp_proddesc_0?ie=UTF8&n=290380&s=music&isInIframe=0">    
            Alle Produktbeschreibungen</a>
        
      
      
    
    </div>

<!-- Used to set table width because AUI is overriding the width attribute of the tables coming in description -->
<script type="text/javascript">
P.when('jQuery').execute(function($){
    $("#productDescription table").each(function() {
        var width = $(this).attr('width');
        if (width) width += 'px';
        else width = 'auto';
        $(this).css('width', width);

        var padding = $(this).attr('cellpadding');
        if (padding) padding += 'px';
        else padding = '0px';
        $(this).css('padding', padding);
    });
});
</script>

<h3 class="a-spacing-small">Top-Kundenrezensionen</h3>
<div id="revMHRL" class="a-section"> 



























<div id="rev-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R1DD84FMRZ16ML" class="a-section celwidget"><div class="a-row a-spacing-micro"><div class="a-icon-row a-spacing-none"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" title="5.0 von 5 Sternen" href="http://www.amazon.de/review/R1DD84FMRZ16ML/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/276-6773562-8584968?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00000B5LO&channel=detail-glance&nodeID=290380&store=music"><i class="a-icon a-icon-star a-star-5"><span class="a-icon-alt">5.0 von 5 Sternen</span></i></a><span class="a-letter-space"></span><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.de/review/R1DD84FMRZ16ML/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/276-6773562-8584968?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00000B5LO&channel=detail-glance&nodeID=290380&store=music"><span class="a-size-base a-text-bold">Mein Klassiker</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">



  <span class="a-size-normal">
    <span class="a-color-secondary">
      Von
    </span>
    Ein Kunde
  </span>
<span class="a-color-secondary"> am 27. November 2002</span></span></div><div id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R1DD84FMRZ16ML" class="a-row a-spacing-small"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Format: Audio CD</span>






<div class="a-section">
  <span class="MHRHead">Das eigentliche Erfolgsgeheimnis des gleichnamigen Filmklassikers ist unumstritten die Musik. Auch ohne Bilder wird man in die Welt der kubanischen Bars versetzt und die entspannte karribische Lebensart &uuml;bertr&auml;gt sich auf die Zuh&ouml;rer. Die Musik l&auml;&szlig;t sich nicht nur beim aktiven Zuh&ouml;ren geniessen, sondern eignet sich dar&uuml;ber hinaus in geradezu idealer Weise als Hintergrundmusik f&uuml;r gem&uuml;tliche Abende mit Freunden.<br>Ein wesentlicher Teil der Faszination, den diese CD aus&uuml;bt, sind die Musiker selbst. In einer Zeit der geklonten Teenie-Stars und Boybands, die entsprechend der neuesten Trends aus der Retorte geschaffen werden und in aberwitzigen B&uuml;hneshows durch die Gegend h&uuml;pfen, ist es eine wahre Wohltat diesen Musiker-Orginalen zuzuh&ouml;ren.<br>Dem aus Amerika stammenden Gitarristen Ry Cooder merkt man f&ouml;rmlich die Begeisterung an, mit der er die St&uuml;cke spielt. Die flinken Finger des Pianisten Rub&eacute;n Gonz&aacute;lez, der damals bereits &uuml;ber 80 Jahre alt war, sind ein Erlebnis f&uuml;r sich. Dazu die tiefe herbe und zugleich melodische Stimme des &uuml;ber 90 Jahre alte Compay Segundo und die melancholisch angehauchte Stimme von Ibrahim Ferrer verspr&uuml;hen einen unvergleichlichen Charme und zeugen vom Charakter und Charisma dieser Musiker.<br>Man bekommt definitiv das Gef&uuml;hl, das hier nicht eine weitere komerzielle CD entstanden ist, sondern das hier echte Gef&uuml;hle und Begeisterung im "Spiel" sind. Dadurch ist die CD auch f&uuml;r Zuh&ouml;rer geeignet, die sich bisher mit derartiger Musik nicht auseinander gesetzt haben. Ich habe bisher noch niemanden erlebt, der von dieser CD ent&auml;uscht gewesen w&auml;re.</span><span class="a-declarative" data-action="columnbalancing-showfullreview" data-columnbalancing-showfullreview="{&quot;rest&quot;:&quot;&lt;br /&gt;Das H&amp;ouml;ren der CD verbreitet eine entspannte Stimmung und weckt die Sehnsucht nach einem Glas Rum und einem Sonnenuntergang auf Kuba. F&amp;uuml;r alle die daf&amp;uuml;r leider keine Zeit haben, ist diese Musik wohl die beste M&amp;ouml;glichkeit in dieses Feeling einzutauchen und sozusagen fast wie ein kleiner Urlaub.&quot;}"><a class="a-link-normal" href="http://www.amazon.de/product-reviews/B00000B5LO/ref=cm_cr_dp_text/276-6773562-8584968?ie=UTF8&showViewpoints=0&sortBy=helpful#R1DD84FMRZ16ML"><span class="a-letter-space"></span>Lesen Sie weiter... &rsaquo;</a></span>

<div id="rev-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R950J3MANF6B6" class="a-section celwidget"><div class="a-row a-spacing-micro"><div class="a-icon-row a-spacing-none"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" title="5.0 von 5 Sternen" href="http://www.amazon.de/review/R950J3MANF6B6/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/276-6773562-8584968?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00000B5LO&channel=detail-glance&nodeID=290380&store=music"><i class="a-icon a-icon-star a-star-5"><span class="a-icon-alt">5.0 von 5 Sternen</span></i></a><span class="a-letter-space"></span><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.de/review/R950J3MANF6B6/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/276-6773562-8584968?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00000B5LO&channel=detail-glance&nodeID=290380&store=music"><span class="a-size-base a-text-bold">Wie von einem anderen Stern</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">
    







  <span class="a-size-normal">
    <span class="a-color-secondary">
      Von
    </span>
    <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/AQ7WAQ8E9J6G8/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp/276-6773562-8584968" class="noTextDecoration">Oliver Klein</a>
  </span>
<span class="a-color-secondary"> am 31. Juli 2002</span></span></div><div id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R950J3MANF6B6" class="a-row a-spacing-small"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Format: Audio CD</span>






<div class="a-section">
  <span class="MHRHead">Hin und wieder brauche ich ein paar neue Anst&ouml;&szlig;e, um meinen musikalischen Horizont zu erweitern. Auf der Suche nach solchen Impulsen bin ich vor einigen Jahren auf den Wim Wenders-Film &quot;Buena Vista Social Club&quot; gesto&szlig;en, der sich dokumentarisch mit dem Leben mehrerer kubanischer Musiker besch&auml;ftigte. Die Musik, in erster Linie als &quot;Son&quot; bekannt, begeisterte mich derma&szlig;en, dass ich beschloss, mich eingehender mit ihr zu besch&auml;ftigen. Was mich am meisten an ihr beeindruckt, ist die Lebensfreude, die sie ausstrahlt. W&auml;hrend reiche und &uuml;bers&auml;ttigte europ&auml;ische und nordamerikanische Musiker gerne schon mal auf Weltschmerz machen, ist der vorliegenden Musik die lebensbejahende Einstellung ihrer Interpreten anzumerken. Und das, obwohl sie traditionsgem&auml;&szlig; ja eher von armen, am Existenzminimum lebenden Menschen geschrieben und gespielt wurde. Davon k&ouml;nnen wir uns vielleicht eine Scheibe abschneiden, wenn wir in unseren Industriestaaten dar&uuml;ber meckern, wie grausam die Welt doch ist und uns beim Abendbrot die neuesten Bilder von den Krisenherden dieser Erde regungs- und kommentarlos anschauen, um danach &uuml;ber die ansteigenden Benzinpreise zu meckern.<br>All dies sp&uuml;rt man nicht auf der CD. Mir scheint sie wie von einem anderen Stern. Die &quot;Einfachheit&quot; der Menschen, die diese Musik machen, hat etwas herzhaft Erfrischendes, was der Musik aus unserem Kulturkreis doch h&auml;ufig abgeht.<br>Und dann ist da noch die Virtuosit&auml;t der alten Herren zu erw&auml;hnen. Die scheinbare Leichtigkeit, mit der sie ihre Instrumente spielen und auch technisch anspruchsvolle Passagen mit links erledigen.</span><span class="a-declarative" data-action="columnbalancing-showfullreview" data-columnbalancing-showfullreview="{&quot;rest&quot;:&quot; Besonders beeindruckt hat mich in diesem Zusammenhang der Pianist Rub&amp;eacute;n Gonz&amp;aacute;lez, der, damals schon &amp;uuml;ber 80j&amp;auml;hrig, die flinken Finger eines Teenagers zu haben scheint.&lt;br /&gt;Unereicht ist auch der &amp;uuml;ber 90 Jahre alte Compay Segundo, dessen lausbubenhafter Charme und Charisma sehr einnehmend sind.&lt;br /&gt;Das einzige st&amp;ouml;rende Element sind Ry Cooders Slidegitarreneinlagen, die irgendwie fehl am Platze wirken - ist aber kaum der Rede wert.&lt;br /&gt;Wer sich die CD kauft, sollte sich &amp;uuml;ber kurz oder lang auch mal mit dem gleichnamigen Film besch&amp;auml;ftigen, denn er macht es leichter, die Zusammenh&amp;auml;nge zu verstehen und veranschaulicht die Lebensumst&amp;auml;nde und den Werdegang der Musiker auf eine gut nachvollziehbare Weise.&quot;}"><a class="a-link-normal" href="http://www.amazon.de/product-reviews/B00000B5LO/ref=cm_cr_dp_text/276-6773562-8584968?ie=UTF8&showViewpoints=0&sortBy=helpful#R950J3MANF6B6"><span class="a-letter-space"></span>Lesen Sie weiter... &rsaquo;</a></span>

<div id="rev-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R2Z4VW0L7G9N7U" class="a-section celwidget"><div class="a-row a-spacing-micro"><div class="a-icon-row a-spacing-none"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" title="5.0 von 5 Sternen" href="http://www.amazon.de/review/R2Z4VW0L7G9N7U/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/276-6773562-8584968?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00000B5LO&channel=detail-glance&nodeID=290380&store=music"><i class="a-icon a-icon-star a-star-5"><span class="a-icon-alt">5.0 von 5 Sternen</span></i></a><span class="a-letter-space"></span><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.de/review/R2Z4VW0L7G9N7U/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/276-6773562-8584968?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00000B5LO&channel=detail-glance&nodeID=290380&store=music"><span class="a-size-base a-text-bold">einfach nur sch&ouml;n.</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">



  <span class="a-size-normal">
    <span class="a-color-secondary">
      Von
    </span>
    Ein Kunde
  </span>
<span class="a-color-secondary"> am 12. Dezember 1999</span></span></div><div id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R2Z4VW0L7G9N7U" class="a-row a-spacing-small"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Format: Audio CD</span>






<div class="a-section">
  Am Anfang habe ich mich noch gefragt, warum alle diesen auf Kuba spielenden Film so toll finden, der doch nur von einigen alten Musikern handelt. Jetzt komme ich von der Filmmusik von Buena Vista Social Club  nicht mehr los. Ry Cooder hat eine wirklich sch&ouml;ne CD zusammengestellt,  deren Songs einem das Gef&uuml;hl geben, selber in Cuba zu sein und den  einheimischen Musikern zu lauschen. Ich war zwar noch nie in der Karibik,  aber so wie diese Musik r&uuml;berkommt, stelle ich mir das Leben dort vor. Zwar  kann ich kein spanisch, aber daf&uuml;r singe ich stolz die meisten Lieder mit,  angefangen mit &quot;Chan Chan&quot; und insbesondere dann auch  &quot;Candela&quot;. Besonders gegl&uuml;ckt finde ich das liebevoll gestaltete  Booklet zu dieser CD, denn dort wird jeder Song vorgestellt und seine  Geschichte erz&auml;hlt. Die Photos zeigen die Interpreten und vermitteln einen  guten Eindruck von der Art und Weise wie diese Aufnahmen entstanden sind.  Ich kann diese CD nur empfehlen, sie hebt sich wohltuend von den anderen  CDs ab, die die Charts bev&ouml;lkern.  (Dies ist eine Amazon.de an der Uni-Studentenrezension.)

<div id="rev-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-RIDT07BYQTHRQ" class="a-section celwidget"><div class="a-row a-spacing-micro"><div class="a-icon-row a-spacing-none"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" title="5.0 von 5 Sternen" href="http://www.amazon.de/review/RIDT07BYQTHRQ/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/276-6773562-8584968?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00000B5LO&channel=detail-glance&nodeID=290380&store=music"><i class="a-icon a-icon-star a-star-5"><span class="a-icon-alt">5.0 von 5 Sternen</span></i></a><span class="a-letter-space"></span><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.de/review/RIDT07BYQTHRQ/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/276-6773562-8584968?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00000B5LO&channel=detail-glance&nodeID=290380&store=music"><span class="a-size-base a-text-bold">An dieser CD ist was dran!</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">



  <span class="a-size-normal">
    <span class="a-color-secondary">
      Von
    </span>
    Ein Kunde
  </span>
<span class="a-color-secondary"> am 12. Januar 2000</span></span></div><div id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-RIDT07BYQTHRQ" class="a-row a-spacing-small"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Format: Audio CD</span>






<div class="a-section">
  Da l&auml;uft seit dem vergangenen Jahr so ein Film mit dem Titel &quot;Buena Vista Social Club&quot; in den Kinos und auf einmal rennen alle wie wild hinter der gleichnamigen Filmmusik her. Was ist das Besondere daran?  Kubanische Musik!? Man k&ouml;nnte jedenfalls denken, da&szlig; mit dieser CD ein  neuer Musikstil erfunden wurde. Diese Musik ist aber schon etwa 150 Jahre  alt. Mit dieser CD kann man also Altes neu entdecken. Zwar gibt es auch  noch anderen Interpreten bzw. CDs, doch ist &quot;Buena Vista Social  Club&quot; eine gelungene Zusammenstellung der temperamentvollen Musik aus  der Karibik. Diese handgemachte Musik &uuml;berzeugt durch schwungvolle Rhythmen  und einen lockeren jazzigen Sound. Das Sahneh&auml;ubchen ist mit Sicherheit das  47 Seiten umfassende Booklet, das Songtitel enth&auml;lt und mit Fotoaufnahmen  die Athmosph&auml;re der Musik illustriert. &quot;Buena Vista Social Club&quot;  bringt Abwechslung in die CD-Regale und ist wirklich zu empfehlen.  (Dies ist eine Amazon.de an der Uni-Studentenrezension.)
</div>

</div>

    var suffix         = '._SL500_AA300_.jpg',
        defaultApparel = '._AA300_.jpg',
        imgUrlSplit    = imgUrl.split("._");

    if (imgUrlSplit.length) {
      var prefix = imgUrlSplit[0];
      if ((!pid  && storeName == "books") || pid == "books_display_on_website") {
        if (imgUrl.match("PIsitb-sticker-arrow")){
          var OUID = imgUrl.substr(imgUrl.indexOf('_OU'), 6);
          var lookInsideSticker = '._BO2,204,203,200_PIsitb-sticker-arrow-click,TopRight,35,-76_AA300_SH20'+ OUID +'.jpg';
          urls.push(prefix + lookInsideSticker);
        } else {
          urls.push(prefix + suffix);
        }
      } else if ((!pid && storeName == "apparel") || pid == "apparel_display_on_website") {
          urls.push(prefix + "._SX342_.jpg");
          urls.push(prefix + "._SY445_.jpg");
      } else if ((!pid && storeName == "shoes") || pid == "shoes_display_on_website") {
          urls.push(prefix + "._SX395_.jpg");
          urls.push(prefix + "._SY395_.jpg");
      } else {
        urls.push(prefix + suffix);
      }
    }
  };

  var urls = [],
      numImgsPreload = Math.min(6, imageUrls.length),
      storeName = "music";

  for (var i = 0; i < numImgsPreload; i++){
    var currPid = (pids && pids.length) ? pids[i] : "";
    transformUrl(imageUrls[i], currPid);
  }

  for (var j = 0; j < urls.length; j++) {
    var img = new Image();
    img.src = urls[j];
  }

};


    var win = jQuery(window);
    var feature = jQuery("#purchaseShvl");
    var shvlPresent = feature.length > 0 ? 1:0;
    var lastCheck = 0;
    var pending = 0;
    
    var onScrollPrecache = function() {
      if (pending) {
        return; 
      }
      var lastCheckDiff = new Date().getTime() - lastCheck;
      var checkDelay = (lastCheckDiff < 200 ? 200 - lastCheckDiff : 10);
      pending = 1;
      var u = function() {
        if(shvlPresent && (win.scrollTop() + win.height() > feature.offset().top + 200)) {  
          var p = precacheDetailImages,
              $ = jQuery;
          if (p) {
            var selector = "#purchaseButtonWrapper";
            var imgElems = $(selector).find("a > div > img");
            var pgs, imgs = [], i = imgElems.length;
            while (i-- > 0) {
              imgs[i] = $(imgElems[i]).attr('src');
            }
            p(imgs,pgs);
          }
          // unbind listening on scroll once pre-caching completed
          $(window).unbind('scroll', onScrollPrecache); 
          return;
        }
        pending = 0; //precache not execute yet, wait next invoke
        lastCheck = new Date().getTime();
      };
      setTimeout(u, checkDelay);
      return;
    };
    
    jQuery(window).bind('scroll', onScrollPrecache);
  });
}
</script>

<script type="text/JavaScript">
(function () {
    "use strict";

    var P = (window.AmazonUIPageJS ? AmazonUIPageJS : window.P);

    var enableYBHLink = function() {
        P.when('p13n-sc-jQuery').execute(function($) {
            $("#ybh-link").click(function() {
                $.ajax({
                      url: '/gp/recent-history-footer/external/ybh-handler.html/276-6773562-8584968',
                      type: "POST",
                      timeout: 2000,
                      data: {
                           parentSession    : '276-6773562-8584968',
                           relatedRequestId : '0HK6SERCZPNQZ1A8TWW1',
                           currentPageType  : 'Detail'
                      },
                      dataType: "text",
                      success: function (data, status) {
                           $("#ybh-link").hide();
                           $("#ybh-text-off").hide();
                           $("#ybh-text-on").show();
                      }
                });
            });
        });
    };

    var lazyLoadRHF = function($) {
        var loadCarousel = function(html) {
            P.when('p13n-sc-carousel-init', 'rhf-container')
             .execute(function(carouselInitializer, rhfContainer) {
                rhfContainer.html(html);
                carouselInitializer.init(rhfContainer);
                enableYBHLink();
            });
        };

        var handleSuccess = function(data) {
            if (typeof(data) === 'object' && data.success && data.html) {
                loadCarousel(data.html);
            } else {
                handleError();
            }
        };

        var handleError = function() {
            P.when('rhf-container', 'rhf-error')
             .execute(function(rhfContainer, rhfError) {
                rhfContainer.hide();
                rhfError.show();
            });
        };

        $.ajax({
            url: '/gp/recent-history-footer/external/rhf-handler.html/276-6773562-8584968',
            type: "POST",
            timeout: 5000,
            data: {
                             isAUI : (typeof window.P === 'object' && window.P.AUI_BUILD_DATE) ? 1 : 0,
                     parentSession : '276-6773562-8584968',
                  relatedRequestId : '0HK6SERCZPNQZ1A8TWW1',
                   currentPageType : 'Detail',
                currentSubPageType : 'Glance',
                       excludeASIN : 'QjAwMDAwQjVMTw==',
                          auiDebug : '',
                          rviAsins : '',
                          rhfState : '',
                          rhfAsins : '',
                       noP13NCache : '',
                         recsAsins : '',
                        customerID : '',
                   testRecsFailure : '',
                    weblabTriggers : '',
           contextMetadataOverride : ''
            },
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (data, status) {
                handleSuccess(data);
            },
            error: function (xhr, status) {
                handleError();
            }
        });
    };

    P.when('p13n-sc-jQuery').execute(function($) {
        P.declare('rhf-container', $("#rhf-container"));
        P.declare('rhf-error', $("#rhf-error"));
        P.declare('rhf-frame', $(".rhf-frame"));
    });

    P.when('p13n-sc-jQuery', 'rhf-container', 'rhf-frame',
            'p13n-sc-call-on-visible', 'p13n-sc-carousel-init')
     .execute(function($, rhfContainer, rhfFrame, callOnVisible, carouselInitializer) {
        rhfFrame.show();
        callOnVisible.register(rhfContainer, function () { lazyLoadRHF($); }, { distance: '-400' })
    });

})();
</script>
